## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical kinetics
**Analysis**: This task involves the rate of change of concentration in a chemical reaction, which is a fundamental concept in chemical kinetics. The relationship between concentration and time is typically modeled using differential equations.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order reaction: dA_dt = -c0 (first-order decay)
- First-order reaction: dA_dt = -c0 * A (exponential decay)
- Second-order reaction: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular reaction)

- Integrated rate law: A(t) = A0 * exp(-c0 * t) (solution to a first-order reaction differential equation)
- Lambert-Weber law: A(t) = c0 / (t**c1 + c2) (growth curve with saturation)
- F1(t) = c0 + c1 * t + c2 * t**2 (second-order reaction, with respect to t)
- A^' = c0 * A * (1 - A/K) (Hill-type growth equation)
- Concentration-dependent reaction rate: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * A) (temperature-independent rate law)
- Concentration-dependent diffusion: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 + c2 * A) (concentration-dependent diffusion coefficient)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs

- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Growth/decay → exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c (growth/decay behavior in chemical reactions)

- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions (threshold concentrations for chemical reactions)
- Reaction saturation: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 / (c1 + c2 * A**2) (saturated reaction rates with respect to concentration)
- Concentration-dependent viscosity: μ = c0 * A / (c1 + c2 * A) (concentration-dependent viscosity)

### Candidate 1:
`(A^(3/2)*c0 + √A*c1 + A³*c2 + A²*c3 + A²*c4 + A²*c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + A*c8 + A*c9*sin(A*c6+c7))/A^(3/2)`

- A^(3/2)*c0/A^(3/2) = c0
- √A*c1/A^(3/2) = c1/A
- A³*c2/A^(3/2) = A^(3/2)*c2
- A²*(c3+c4)/A^(3/2) = √A*(c3+c4)
- A²*c5*sin/A^(3/2) = √A*c5*sin(A*c6+c7)
- A*c8/A^(3/2) = c8/√A
- A*c9*sin/A^(3/2) = c9*sin(A*c6+c7)/√A

To get -0.10017√A + 0.47149*sin(0.85551*A), I need: c0=0, c1=0, c2=0, c3+c4=-0.10017, c8=0. Then I have √A*c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c9*sin(A*c6+c7)/√A. This gives sin(A*c6+c7)*(c5*√A + c9/√A), which is NOT the same as a pure sin term (it has √A dependence multiplied by sin). No match.

√A*(A*c0+c1+A²*c2*c4+A*c3*c4+A*c2*c5*sin+c3*c5*sin) + c8*A*c2+c8*c3

Let me try setting c2=0 to simplify: denominator becomes A+c3.
Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+c3*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*c3
= √A*(A*c0+c1+A*c3*c4+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*c3
= √A*(A*(c0+c3*c4)+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*c3

Dividing by (A+c3):
[A^(3/2)*(c0+c3*c4)+√A*(c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*c3]/(A+c3)

This is complex. Let me try c0+c3*c4=0 (so c0=-c3*c4):
[√A*(c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*c3]/(A+c3)

Still doesn't simplify to √A + sin form easily. Let me try another approach: set c3=0.
Denominator: A. Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+A*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*0 (wait, c8*(A*c2+c3)=c8*(A*c2+0)=c8*A*c2, but c2=0 already... so c8*0=0).

With c2=0, c3=0: denominator=A, numerator=√A*(A*c0+c1+0)=√A*(A*c0+c1)=A^(3/2)*c0+√A*c1.
Result: √A*c0+c1/√A. Not matching (1/√A ≠ sin).

Let me try differently. Set c4=0:
Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+(A*c2+c3)*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*(A*c2+c3)
Denominator: A+c3

If I also set c2=0:
Num: √A*(A*c0+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*c3
Den: A+c3

For this to equal -0.10017√A+0.47149*sin(0.85551*A):
(-0.10017√A+0.47149*sin(0.85551*A))*(A+c3) = √A*(A*c0+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*c3

LHS: -0.10017*A^(3/2)-0.10017*c3*√A+0.47149*A*sin(0.85551*A)+0.47149*c3*sin(0.85551*A)

RHS: A^(3/2)*c0+√A*c1+√A*c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7)+c8*c3

Matching A^(3/2): c0=-0.10017
Matching √A: c1=-0.10017*c3
Matching A*sin(0.85551*A): coefficient 0.47149 on LHS, but on RHS there's no A*sin term. This fails.

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4:
`√A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + (c0+c4*sin(A*c5+c6))*(A*c7+c8)`

Expanding: √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c0*A*c7+c0*c8+c4*A*c7*sin(A*c5+c6)+c4*c8*sin(A*c5+c6)

To match GT, set c7=0: √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c0*c8 + c4*c8*sin(A*c5+c6)

Set c4=0 (or c8 chosen appropriately): √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c0*c8

This gives √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + constant. GT has no constant. But wait, we can set c8=0:
√A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + 0 + 0 = √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3)

With c0=-0.10017, c1=0.47149, c2=0.85551, c3=0: this matches GT!

Candidate 4 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 5:
`√A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c4*(c0+c5*sin(A*c6+c7))*sin(A*c8+c9)`

Set c4=0: √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3). This matches GT with appropriate constants.

Candidate 5 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 6:
`(A*c0+c1*(A*c2+c3)*log(A*c4+1)+c5+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c6+c7*sin(A*c8)))/(A*c2+c3)`

= A*c0/(A*c2+c3) + c1*log(A*c4+1) + c5/(A*c2+c3) + A*c6 + c7*sin(A*c8)

Setting c1=0, c6=0: A*c0/(A*c2+c3) + c5/(A*c2+c3) + c7*sin(A*c8)
= (A*c0+c5)/(A*c2+c3) + c7*sin(A*c8)

The rational part is a ratio of linear functions in A, which can be a constant + constant/A type. It cannot produce √A. No match.

Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 7:
`A^(5/2)*c0 + A^(3/2)*c1 + A^(3/2)*c2*sin(A*c3+c4) + A^(3/2)*c5 + √A*c6 + √A*c7*sin(A*c3+c4) + A*c8 + c9`

Set c0=0, c1=0, c2=0, c5=0, c8=0, c9=0: √A*c6 + √A*c7*sin(A*c3+c4)
= √A*(c6+c7*sin(A*c3+c4))

This gives √A*c6 + √A*c7*sin(A*c3+c4). GT needs √A + sin(A*c), but here the sin term is multiplied by √A. These are different basis functions: √A*sin(A*c) ≠ sin(A*c). No match.

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 8:
`(A*c0+c1*(A*c2+c3)*exp(A*c4)+c5+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c6+c7*sin(A*c8+c9)))/(A*c2+c3)`

= A*c0/(A*c2+c3) + c1*exp(A*c4) + c5/(A*c2+c3) + A*c6 + c7*sin(A*c8+c9)

Setting c1=0, c6=0: (A*c0+c5)/(A*c2+c3) + c7*sin(A*c8+c9). Rational function of A + sin. Can't produce √A.

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 9:
`√A*c0*sin(A*c1+c2) + c3*sin(A*c4)`

Basis functions: √A*sin(A*c) and sin(A*c). GT needs √A and sin(A*c). √A*sin ≠ √A (unless sin=constant, but then it's constant*√A and we lose the sin term). If c0=0: just c3*sin(A*c4), missing √A. Can't match both terms.

Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 10:
`√A*c0 + c1*cos(A*c2+c3)`

cos(A*c2+c3) = cos(c3)*cos(A*c2) - sin(c3)*sin(A*c2). With c3 = -π/2: cos(A*c2-π/2) = sin(A*c2).

So this becomes √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2), which matches GT with c0=-0.10017, c1=0.47149, c2=0.85551.

Candidate 10 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 11:
`√A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2)`

Directly: √A*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2). Set c0=-0.10017, c1=0.47149, c2=0.85551. Perfect match.

Candidate 11 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 12:
`A*c0*exp(A*c1) + c2*sin(A*c3) + c4*log(A*c5+1) + c6*exp(A*c7)`

Set c0=0, c4=0, c6=0: c2*sin(A*c3). Missing √A. 
Set c1=0: c0*A + c2*sin(A*c3) + c4*log(A*c5+1) + c6*exp(A*c7). 
Can't produce √A from A, log, exp, sin combinations. No match.

Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 13:
`(c0*(A*c1+c2)+(A*c3+1)*(A*c4+c5+(A+c2)*(A*c6+c7*sin(A*c8+c9))))/((A*c1+c2)*(A*c3+1))`

= c0/(A*c3+1) + (A*c4+c5+(A+c2)*(A*c6+c7*sin(A*c8+c9)))/(A*c1+c2)

Expanding (A+c2)*(A*c6+c7*sin) = A²*c6+A*c7*sin+A*c2*c6+c2*c7*sin

So numerator of second part: A*c4+c5+A²*c6+A*c7*sin(A*c8+c9)+A*c2*c6+c2*c7*sin(A*c8+c9)

All rational functions of A. Can't produce √A. No match.

Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14:
`(A*(A*c0+A*c1+c2*exp(A*c3)+c4*sin(A*c5+c6)+c7)+c8+c9*sin(A*c5+c6))/A`

= A*(c0+c1) + c2*exp(A*c3) + c4*sin(A*c5+c6) + c7 + c8/A + c9*sin(A*c5+c6)/A

Basis: A, exp, sin, constant, 1/A, sin/A. No √A. No match.

Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 15:
`(A*c0+c1*(A*c2+c3)*log(A*c4+1)+c5+(A+c3)*(A*c6+c7*sin(A*c8+c9)))/(A*c2+c3)`

Note the numerator has (A+c3) not (A*c2+c3). Let me expand:
= A*c0/(A*c2+c3) + c1*log(A*c4+1) + c5/(A*c2+c3) + (A+c3)*(A*c6+c7*sin(A*c8+c9))/(A*c2+c3)

If c2=1: denominator = A+c3, and (A+c3)*(A*c6+c7*sin)/(A+c3) = A*c6+c7*sin(A*c8+c9).
Then: A*c0/(A+c3) + c1*log(A*c4+1) + c5/(A+c3) + A*c6 + c7*sin(A*c8+c9)

Setting c1=0, c6=0: (A*c0+c5)/(A+c3) + c7*sin(A*c8+c9). Rational + sin. No √A.

Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 16:
`c0*(A+c1)*exp(A*c2) + c3*cos(A*c4+c5) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1)+c9)`

sin(c7*log(A*c8+1)+c9) - can this equal √A? log and sin composition can't produce √A for all A. No match.

Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 17:

### Candidate 18:

### Candidate 20:
`(√A*(A*c0+c1+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*(A*c2+c3))/(√A*(A+c3))`

Compare with Candidate 3 but denominator is √A*(A+c3) instead of (A+c3).

Let me set c2=0: denominator = √A*(A+c3)
Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+c3*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*c3
= √A*(A*(c0+c3*c4)+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+c8*c3

Dividing by √A*(A+c3):
= (A*(c0+c3*c4)+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))/(A+c3) + c8*c3/(√A*(A+c3))

This gives rational functions and 1/√A terms. Can we get √A from this?

Let me try c2=1, so denominator = √A*(A+c3), and (A*c2+c3) = A+c3.
Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+(A+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*(A+c3)
= √A*(A*c0+c1+A²*c4+A*c3*c4+A*c5*sin+c3*c5*sin)+c8*A+c8*c3

Dividing by √A*(A+c3):
= (A*c0+c1+A²*c4+A*c3*c4+A*c5*sin+c3*c5*sin)/(A+c3) + c8/√A + c8*c3/(√A*(A+c3))

Hmm, this gives 1/√A terms but not √A. Let me try yet another approach.

Set c3=0: denominator = √A*A = A^(3/2). Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+A*c2*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+0
= √A*(A*c0+c1+A²*c2*c4+A*c2*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))

Dividing by A^(3/2): (A*c0+c1+A²*c2*c4+A*c2*c5*sin)/(A)
= c0+c1/A+A*c2*c4+c2*c5*sin(A*c6+c7)

Setting c2*c4=0 (say c4=0): c0+c1/A+c2*c5*sin(A*c6+c7). No √A.

This structure can't produce √A. No match.

Candidate 20 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 21:
`A²*c0*exp(A*c1) + c2*sin(A*c3+c4) + c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7*log(c8*exp(A*c9)+1)`

### Candidate 24:
`(√A*(A*c0+c1+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+A*c8)/(√A*(A*c2+c3))`

Set c2=0: denominator = √A*c3. Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+c3*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+A*c8
= √A*(A*(c0+c3*c4)+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))+A*c8

Dividing by √A*c3:
= (A*(c0+c3*c4)+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))/c3 + A*c8/(√A*c3)
= A*(c0+c3*c4)/c3 + c1/c3 + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8*√A/c3

So we get: constant*A + constant + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + (c8/c3)*√A

Setting c0+c3*c4=0 (i.e., c0=-c3*c4) and c1=0:
c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + (c8/c3)*√A

This matches GT! Set c8/c3 = -0.10017, c5 = 0.47149, c6 = 0.85551, c7 = 0.

Candidate 24 verdict: [MATCH]

### Candidate 25:
`A*c0*exp(A*c1) + c2*sin(A*c3+c4) + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8*log(A*c9+1)`

### Candidate 30:
`(c0*t+c1-(c2*t+c3)*(c4*(A+c5)*exp(A*c6)+c7*sin(A*c8+c9)))/(c3+t)`

This depends on t. Setting c0=0, c2=0: (c1-c3*(c4*(A+c5)*exp(A*c6)+c7*sin(A*c8+c9)))/(c3+t)

Still has t in denominator. Setting c0=c2=0 and looking at the structure: c1/(c3+t) - c3*f(A)/(c3+t). This always depends on t unless we can eliminate t. 

If c0/c2 = c1/c3 (so that numerator factors): Let c0 = k*c2, c1 = k*c3. Then numerator = k*(c2*t+c3) - (c2*t+c3)*(c4*(A+c5)*exp(A*c6)+c7*sin(A*c8+c9)) = (c2*t+c3)*(k - c4*(A+c5)*exp(A*c6) - c7*sin(A*c8+c9)).

Denominator is c3+t. So result = (c2*t+c3)/(c3+t) * (k - ...). If c2=1: (t+c3)/(c3+t) = 1. Then result = k - c4*(A+c5)*exp(A*c6) - c7*sin(A*c8+c9). 

Setting c4=0: k - c7*sin(A*c8+c9). This is constant + sin. No √A. No match.

Candidate 30 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 41:
`(√A*(A*c0+c1+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8)/(√A*(A*c2+c3))`

Similar to Candidate 24 but with c8 instead of A*c8.

Set c2=0: denominator = √A*c3. Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+c3*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8

= A*(c0+c3*c4)/c3 + c1/c3 + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8/(c3*√A)

Setting c0+c3*c4=0, c1=0: c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8/(c3*√A)

This gives sin + 1/√A. But GT needs sin + √A. 1/√A ≠ √A. No match.

### Candidate 43:
`(√A*(A*c0+c1+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*(A*c2+c3))/(√A*(A*c2+c3))`

This is the same as Candidate 20! Let me re-examine.

Denominator: √A*(A*c2+c3). Set c2=0: √A*c3.
Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+c3*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*c3

Dividing: (A*(c0+c3*c4)+c1+c3*c5*sin(A*c6+c7))/c3 + c8*c3/(√A*c3)
= A*(c0+c3*c4)/c3 + c1/c3 + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8/√A

Setting c0+c3*c4=0, c1=0: c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8/√A

This gives sin + 1/√A, not sin + √A. 

Wait, let me try a different approach. What if c2≠0?

Let me try to see if we can get √A. The full expression:
= (A*c0+c1)/(√A*(A*c2+c3)) + A*c4/√A + c5*sin(A*c6+c7)/√A + c8/√A

Wait, let me redo this more carefully.

Numerator: √A*(A*c0+c1+(A*c2+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)))+c8*(A*c2+c3)

Let me expand (A*c2+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin) = A²*c2*c4+A*c3*c4+A*c2*c5*sin+c3*c5*sin

So numerator = √A*(A*c0+c1+A²*c2*c4+A*c3*c4+A*c2*c5*sin+c3*c5*sin)+c8*A*c2+c8*c3
= A^(5/2)*c2*c4 + A^(3/2)*(c0+c3*c4+c2*c5*sin) + √A*(c1+c3*c5*sin) + c8*A*c2+c8*c3

Wait, the sin depends on A so I can't factor it out like that. Let me be more careful.

Numerator = √A*A*c0 + √A*c1 + √A*(A*c2+c3)*(A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7)) + c8*(A*c2+c3)

Denominator = √A*(A*c2+c3)

Dividing: A*c0/(A*c2+c3) + c1/(A*c2+c3) + A*c4+c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8/√A

So the result is: A*c0/(A*c2+c3) + c1/(A*c2+c3) + A*c4 + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + c8/√A

We have: rational function of A + linear in A + sin + 1/√A.

To match GT = √A*k1 + k2*sin(k3*A), we need the rational and linear parts to combine to give √A, which is impossible since rational functions and polynomials can't produce √A. And c8/√A ≠ √A.
